b'March is being observed as Fire Prevention Month here in the Philippines\xe2\x80\x93a perfect time to discuss and raise awareness about the causes, hazards, and dangers of fire.\n\nBy virtue of Proclamation No. 115-A, signed by then-President Ferdinand E. Marcos, and Proclamation No. 360 in 1986, the month of March was declared as \xe2\x80\x9cFire Prevention Month\xe2\x80\x9d or \xe2\x80\x9cBurn Prevention Month.\xe2\x80\x9d\n\nThe fire prevention month campaign, according to the measure, promotes \xe2\x80\x9csafety consciousness among our people every day of the year as a positive preventive approach to a problem that can be solved by more caution, vigilance, sobriety, the exercise of common sense, and respect for the law.\xe2\x80\x9d\n\nState weather bureau PAGASA said the temperature and humidity in March start to reach higher levels, with the hot, dry weather causing a rise in reported fire cases around the country.\n\nMarch is one of the hottest months of the year and it marks the beginning of the summer season in the Philippines. It is also the month that has one of the most alarming fire incidents in the country, based on data by the Bureau of Fire Protection (BFP).\n\nAs we observe this advocacy campaign, we should exercise vigilance and be more aware and knowledgeable about fire prevention to keep ourselves and our family safe.\n\nTo make sure that your family and house are safe, the BFP recommends these tips to avoid the occurrence of fire:\n1.) Unplug all electrical equipment when not in use and regularly check electrical equipment to avoid overloading of electrical circuits.\n2.) When using cooking gas, check for gas leaks and always ensure that the LPG tank is stored in a well-ventilated area to avoid the accumulation of gas vapors.\n3.) Enforce \xe2\x80\x9cNo Smoking\xe2\x80\x9d policy inside or outside the house and dispose of cigarette butts properly.\n4.) Practice proper housekeeping and keep flammable materials out of reach of children. Flammable materials include candles, lighters, and matches, which should be kept properly and securely.\n5.) Plan ahead\xe2\x80\x93establish an emergency and evacuation plan at home and familiarize with escape routes. And most importantly, keep flammables away from your children\n6.) In case of fire, close the door of the burning area to stop the spread of fire. As smoke rises up, breathe slowly, and get a piece of wet cloth to cover the nose and mouth to avoid suffocation.\n7.) When trapped in a fire hit area, it is highly recommended to go to a room with windows leading outdoors.\n8.) If clothes catch fire, do not run or panic, do the: \xe2\x80\x9cStop, Drop, and Roll. \xe2\x80\x9cIn this life-threatening situation, shout for help or wave a cloth outside the window to alert the people around you and keep in mind to remain calm.\n9.) The most important thing to do is to call 911, the nationwide emergency hotline number, and tell the emergency operator of your location right away.\nFire incidents are potentially deadly and very dangerous, but by following these safety precautions from authorities, we can prevent untoward incidents from happening. Just remember that having the presence of mind in any situation can also spell the difference between being a victim and being a fire survivor.\nIn line with educating the public on fire prevention, the BFP also encourages everyone to get involved and actively participate in fire drills conducted by barangays, schools, place of employment, and local government units. Fire drills are essential and allows everyone the chance to rehearse proper evacuation procedures. These also train participants to behave rationally amidst the crisis. Keep safe. (CA/PIA-Infocomm)\n Source: https://prri.da.gov.ph/fire-prevention-month/\n#FirePreventionMonth\n#ISELCO2'

b'Ipinapaalam ng pamunuan ng ISELCO II na ang bahagyang pagtaas ng taripa ng kuryente ay dulot ng  pagbabalik ng Feed-in Tariffs Allowance o FIT ALL Tariffs na ipinapataw ng NGCP sa lahat ng MCOs sa pamamagitan ng mga Electric Cooperatives sa buong Pilipinas. b'\xe2\x9a\xa1POWER ADVISORY UPDATE\xe2\x9a\xa1\n As of January 19, 2024 | 01:45 PM\n\xf0\x9f\x92\xa1ENERGIZED\xf0\x9f\x92\xa1'
b'Isang mabuting balita muli ang hatid ng Kooperatiba para sa mga MCOs!\nMuli pang bumaba ang taripa ng kuryente na ipatutupad ng ISELCO II ngayong buwan ng Enero 2024. 9.5280/kwh ang para sa mga residential consumers, habang 8.3377/kwh sa low voltage, 7.0845/kwh sa high voltage, at  10.0825/kwh sa SPUG PALANAN.\n\nMatatandaan na ang pagpapababa sa taripa ng kuryente ay isa sa mga pangunahing layunin ni Acting General Manager, Engr. Erni Baggao na siya pa ring nangunguna sa patuloy na pakikipagtulungan sa pamahalaang panlalawigan at pakikipag-ugnayan sa mga power suppliers upang makapaghatid ng sapat na supply ng kuryente sa mas mababang halaga. Batid ni Engr. Baggao na ang presyo ng kuryente ay isa sa mga iniinda ng mga MCOs na nais niyang tugunan mula nang siya pa lamang ay nagsimulang umupo bilang AGM ng Kooperatiba.\n\nMuli ay nagpapaabot ng pasasalamat si AGM Baggao sa  lahat ng mga member-consumers na patuloy na nagtitiwala at sumusuporta sa Kooperatiba. Makakaasa ang mga MCOs sa kanyang patuloy na pagsusumikap upang maitaguyod at maiangat pa lalo ang ISELCO II para sa ikabubuti ng mga consumers.\n#JanuaryPowerRate\n#ISELCO2'

b'10 days to go before the 40th Annual General Membership Assembly.\nCome and Attend to get a chance of winning exciting raffle prizes.\nOn January 28, 2024 | SUNDAY | 8:00 AM\nRudy B. Albano Astrodome, Tumauini Isabela.\n\n#ISELCODOS\n#40thAGMA\n#AGMA2024'
b'Day 2: The Employee Engagement Seminar, and Labor & Employee Education Seminar concluded today at the Piazza Zicarelli Hotel and Resort, Brgy. Upi, Gamu, Isabela. The seminar is in collaboration with the Department of Labor and Employment (DOLE - Region 02).\n\nThe training sets out to provide a comprehensive overview on the latest developments and emerging trends in labor and employment laws thereby equipping the participants with the knowledge and tools that will help them navigate the complexities of the modern workplace in a rapidly changing global lanscape.\n\nThe discussion on the final day  was directed by DOLE-Senior Labor & Employment Officer / Labor Relations Unit Head, Ms. Divine Grace P. Cristobal; DOLE - Assistant Labor Inspector III of Isabela Field Office, Mr. Romeo Solomon A. Sales Jr., and lastly, DOLE - Assistant Labor Inspector II of Isabela Field Office Engr. Ron Oliver B. Tagude. \n\nThe topics discussed were centered on Management Prerogative, General Labor Standards, and Occupational Safety & Health which highlighted the duties and responsibilities of  Labor Union Officers, Management, and Staff. During the seminar, the employees made the most out of the opportunity to deepen their understanding of labor law by fostering an environment of open dialogue, mutual respect and collaboration.\n#LaborEmploymentEducationSeminar\n#ISELCO2'
b'TODAY | ISABELA II ELECTRIC COOPERATIVE (ISELCO II) in partnership with Regional Tripitate Wages & Productivity Board (RTWPB -Region 2) conducted Employee Engagement Seminar at Piazza Zicarelli Hotel, Highway, Gamu, Isabela. \n\nThe resource speakers during the employee engagement seminar were representative from Regional Tripartite Wages and Productivity Board Region 2 ( RTWPB R02 ) in the person of Atty. Lovely Mei Delacruz,  Atty IV and Mr. Francis Joseph Reyes Information Technology Officer I, both of RTWPB R02. The objective of the said seminar is to involve employees to be enthusiastic and efficient to their work and to their working environment.\n\nThis is a great and useful seminar allowing heads, managers and employees to find out more about employee engagement, and how to make the most of their greatest asset throughout year.\n\n#ISELCO2'

(CAGELCO II), Isabela I Electric Cooperative, Inc.(ISELCO I), Isabela II Electric Cooperative (ISELCO II), Nueva Vizcaya Electric Cooperative (NUVELCO), Quirino Electric Cooperative (QUIRELCO), and Batanes Electric Cooperative (BATANELCO).\n\nBoard of Directors, General Managers and Employees from the aforementioned cooperatives  gathered at the Mango Suites Hotel, Cauayan City, Isabela on the said date to have fun and celebrate the Christmas season.\n\nThe day commenced with a heartwarming welcome from Isabela II Electric Cooperative Acting General Manager and NAGMEC President R02, Engr. b'LOOK| Last November 28,2023 representatives from the Cooperative Development Authority (CDA) Region 2 namely Mr. John K. Nahpadan and Mr. Ronyl B. Cano, both Cooperative Development Specialists (CDS) conducted annual inspection at the Isabela II Electric Cooperative (ISELCO II). \n\nThe CDA Development Specialists focused on the discussion of provisions related to cooperative development to ensure that cooperatives comply with the regulatory requirements imposed by the cooperative laws, rules and regulations, related legislation, and other administrative issuances.\n\n Whereas, today, November 30, 2023, an exit conference was convened in ISELCO II conference room attended by Department Managers and other key staff to conclude their official business, wherein conclusions, recommendations, and other suggestions for further improvement of the Cooperative were addressed.\n\n#ISELCO2'

b'Isang mabuting balita muli ang hatid ng Kooperatiba para sa mga MCOs!\n\nMuli pang bumaba ang taripa ng kuryente na ipatutupad ng ISELCO II ngayong buwan ng Nobyembre 2023. 9.5336/kwh ang para sa mga residential consumers, habang 8.3433/kwh sa low voltage, 7.2423/kwh sa high voltage, at  9.4614/kwh sa SPUG PALANAN.\n\nMatatandaan na ang pagpapababa sa taripa ng kuryente ay isa sa mga pangunahing layunin ni Acting General Manager, Engr. Erni Baggao na siya pa ring nangunguna sa patuloy na pakikipagtulungan sa pamahalaang panlalawigan at pakikipag-ugnayan sa mga power suppliers upang makapaghatid ng sapat na supply ng kuryente sa mas mababang halaga. Batid ni Engr. Baggao na ang presyo ng kuryente ay isa sa mga iniinda ng mga MCOs na nais niyang tugunan mula nang siya pa lamang ay nagsimulang umupo bilang AGM ng Kooperatiba.\n\nMuli ay nagpapaabot ng pasasalamat si AGM Baggao sa  lahat ng mga member-consumers na patuloy na nagtitiwala at sumusuporta sa Kooperatiba. Makakaasa ang mga MCOs sa kanyang patuloy na pagsusumikap upang maitaguyod at maiangat pa lalo ang ISELCO II para sa ikabubuti ng mga consumers.\n#NovemberPowerRate\n#ISELCO2'

b"November 17, 2023 - The 2nd day of the Cooperative's comprehensive first aid training program focused on teaching participants the essential skills of bandaging and proper carrying techniques. In this training, participants learned the importance of bandages in providing immediate care and stabilizing injuries. They gained hands-on experience in applying different types of bandages, including gauze, triangular, and elastic bandages, to effectively manage wounds, sprains, and fractures.\n\nAdditionally, the training covered the correct methods of carrying injured individuals to ensure their safety and minimize further harm. Participants learned various carrying techniques, such as the two-person seat carry, the clothes drag, and the blanket drag, depending on the situation and the severity of the injury.\n\nOnce again, the cooperative extends its gratitude to the Philippine RedCross and to Mr. Mark Oliver Alimuc & Mr. Lorencio Calde\xc3\xb1a, as well as to ISELCO II's Safety Officer Mr. Henry Pavon, for serving as resource speakers and sharing their invaluable knowledge and skills.\n\n#ISELCO2"

b'Patuloy pa rin ang pagtanggap ng ISELCO II ng applications para sa Lifeline rate discount para sa mga 4Ps at non-4Ps beneficiaries na kumokonsumo ng 1-20 kWh kada buwan. Ang programang ito ay sang-ayon sa Republic Act 11552 o Lifeline Rate Extension Act.\n\nUpang mapabilis ang proseso, ang Kooperatiba ay patuloy pa rin sa pakikipag-ugnayan sa mga Liga ng Barangay sa bawat munisipalidad para sa clustered na pagtanggap ng aplikasyon. Kasabay ng pagtanggap ng application, ang mga kawani ng Kooperatiba na personal na bumibisita sa mga barangay ay nagsasagawa rin ng Information Education and Communication (IEC) campaign upang maipaliwanag ng husto ang nasabing programa. \n\nAng full implementation ng Lifeline Rate Program ay extended hanggang January 1, 2024.\n\n#ISELCO2'

b'October 20, 2023 - Today concludes the 4-day seminar on the Fundamentals of Cooperative and Governance and Cooperative Management at the ISELCO II Main Office Conference room in Alibagu, City of Ilagan, Isabela hosted by the Northeast Luzon Credit Cooperative League - Philippine Federation of Credit Cooperative (NELCCO-PFCCO).\n\nThe purpose of this training program is to inspire and equip the new members of the Committee on Board to strive for excellence in their service to the coop and its members.\n\nThe discussion on the final day of the seminar concentrated on Governance and Management of Cooperative, which highlighted the duties and responsibilities of the Committee on Board.\n#ISELCO2'
b'Isang mabuting balita muli ang hatid ng Kooperatiba para sa mga MCOs!\n\nTuluyan nang bumaba sa single digit ang taripa ng kuryente na ipatutupad ng ISELCO II ngayong buwan ng Oktubre 2023. 9.6560/kwh ang para sa mga residential consumers, habang 8.4657/kwh sa low voltage, at 7.0909/kwh sa high voltage.\n\nMatatandaan na ang pagpapababa sa taripa ng kuryente ay isa sa mga pangunahing layunin ni Acting General Manager, Engr. Erni Baggao na siya pa ring nangunguna sa patuloy na pakikipagtulungan sa pamahalaang panlalawigan at pakikipag-ugnayan sa mga power suppliers upang makapaghatid ng sapat na supply ng kuryente sa mas mababang halaga. Batid ni Engr. Baggao na ang presyo ng kuryente ay isa sa mga iniinda ng mga MCOs na nais niyang tugunan mula nang siya pa lamang ay nagsimulang umupo bilang AGM ng Kooperatiba.\n\nMuli ay nagpapaabot ng pasasalamat si AGM Baggao sa  lahat ng mga member-consumers na patuloy na nagtitiwala at sumusuporta sa Kooperatiba. Makakaasa ang mga MCOs sa kanyang patuloy na pagsusumikap upang maitaguyod at maiangat pa lalo ang ISELCO II para sa ikabubuti ng mga consumers.\n\n#ISELCO2'

b'IN PHOTOS: The ISELCO II management and staff headed by Engr. Erni G. Baggao appeared before the honorable Board Members of the Province of Isabela for a meeting at the Legislative Room of the Isabela Provincial Capitol on September 21, 2023. \n\nPresent at the meeting were ISELCO II Board of Directors chaired by Director Hardy V. Urma, Acting General Manager Engr. Erni G. Bagggao, Department Managers, and other key personnel of ISELCO II.\n\nThe Acting General Manager, Erni G. Baggao reported updates on ISELCO II\xe2\x80\x99s current status, accomplishments in the past nine months since his designation, as well as the Coop\xe2\x80\x99s plans and projects for the benefit of member-consumer-owners. Engr. Baggao also informed the Provincial Board Members of the current Cash-in-bank of the cooperative and the recent decrease in power rate. Moreover, the meeting served as a venue to deliberate the ongoing ERC case on the recovery of ISELCO II to the overcharges billed by the previous power providers of the Cooperative.\n\nAfter the discussion, Engr. Baggao was highly commended by the Provincial Board Members who also affirmed their confidence in his leadership alongside the new set of Board of Directors and the management of ISELCO II.\n#ISELCO2'

b'Magandang balita!\n\nPatuloy ang pagbaba ng power rate na ipatutupad ngayong buwan ng Setyembre 2023. \n\nMula Php 11.8726/kwh noong buwan ng Agosto, ngayong buwan ay Php 10.5497/kwh na lang para sa residential consumers. \n\nMula naman sa Php 10.6823/kwh ay bumaba ito ngayong buwan sa Php 9.3594/kwh para sa low voltage consumers. \n\nHabang ang singil sa high voltage consumers ngayong Setyembre ay Php 8.0266/kwh mula sa dating Php 9.3397/kwh.\n\nKasabay ng magandang balitang ito ay umabot na sa halagang one billion nine million three hundred sixty-five thousand six hundred eighty-six and twenty-four cents (\xe2\x82\xbd1,009,365,686.24) ang naipong pondo ng Kooperatiba ngayong Sept 20, 2023.\n\nIto ay ang kauna-unahang pagkakataon sa kasaysayan ng ISELCO II na nakaipon ng ganito kalaking halaga na kung saan  makatutulong para sa pagpapabuti at pagsasa-ayos pa lalo ng serbisyong pangkuryente para sa mga MCOs ng kooperatiba.\n\nIto ay naisakatuparan sa loob lamang ng siyam na buwan sa  pamumuno ni Acting General Manager, Engr. Erni Baggao.  \n\nAng kasalukuyang pamumuno ni AGM Baggao ay nakatuon sa pagbibigay ng mas abot-kayang taripa ng kuryente para sa mga member-consumer-owners. \n\nBukod pa rito ay tinututukan rin niyang mabuti ang mga plano at programa sa pagpapataas ng collection efficiency at pagbaba ng Systems Loss ng Kooperatiba sapagkat ito ay isa sa mga batayan ng Kooperatibang nasa mabuting estado o katayuan. \n\nMuli ay nagpapaabot ng pasasalamat si AGM Baggao at ang buong pamunuan ng ISELCO II sa  lahat ng mga member-consumers na patuloy na nagtitiwala at sumusuporta sa  ating Kooperatiba.\n#SeptemberPowerRate\n#ISELCO2\n#RoadTo1Billion\n#TargetAchieved'

b"The 2023 Barangay Power Association (BAPA) Summit is yet another successful activity that was conducted by ISABELA II ELECTRIC COOPERATIVE on August 31, 2023 at the Ilagan Community Center, Centro Poblacion, City of Ilagan, Isabela.\n\nThe said activity was graced by ISELCO II's Acting General Manager Engr. Erni G. Baggao, the Board of Directors headed by Chairman Hardy V. Urma, Department Managers, ISELCO II key staff and BAPA officers from the different municipalities within the service area of the Cooperative. \n\nThe BAPA Summit was an opportunity to discuss relevant matters regarding BAPA operations such as the BAPA constitution and By-Laws and the existing policies in effect.\n\nMoreover, the event served as a venue to give rightful recognition to the Best Performing BAPAs in the previous year.\n\nThe Cooperative is truly grateful for the untiring contribution of our BAPAs all over the ISELCO II Coverage Area and is looking forward to do more activities like this to organize and empower them as one of ISELCO II's partners in attaining its cooperative goals.\n#ISELCO2"

b"POWER RATE UPDATE\n\nMagandang balita!\n\nIpatutupad ngayong buwan ng Agosto 2023 ang pagbaba ng power rate mula sa Php 12.3563/kWh noong nakaraang buwan ay bumaba sa Php 11.8726/kwh para sa residential consumers. Mula naman sa Php 11.1660/kWh ay bumaba ito ngayong buwan sa Php 10.6823/kwh para sa low voltage consumers. Habang ang singil sa high voltage consumers ay bumaba ngayong buwan mula Php 9.8056/kWh sa Php 9.3397/kwh.\n\nSa kabila ng abalang iskedyul ng pamunuan ng ISELCO II dahil sa iba't ibang nakahanay na aktibidad ng Kooperatiba, sa pamumuno ni Acting General Manager, Engr. Erni Baggao, ay pinagtuunan pa rin ng pansin at pinagsikapang gumawa ng mga hakbang upang mapababa ang taripa ng kuryente ngayong buwan ng Agosto.\n\nSa kabila nito, patuloy pa rin ang aming paalala na mahalagang maging masinop at matalino sa paggamit ng kuryente.\n\n#AugustPowerRate\n#ISELCO2"

b"POWER RATE UPDATE\n\nMagandang balita!\nIpatutupad ngayong buwan ng Hulyo 2023 ang pagbaba ng power rate mula sa Php 15.3366/kwh noong nakaraang buwan ay bumaba sa Php 12.3563/kwh para sa residential consumers. Mula naman sa Php 14.1463/kwh ay bumaba ito ngayong buwan sa Php 11.1660/kwh para sa low voltage consumers. Habang ang singil sa high voltage consumers ay bumaba ngayong buwan mula Php 12.7432/kwh sa Php 9.8056/kwh.\n\nSa kabila ng abalang iskedyul ng pamunuan ng ISELCO II dahil sa iba't ibang nakahanay na aktibidad ng Kooperatiba, sa pamumuno ni Acting General Manager, Engr., Erni Baggao, ay pinagtuunan pa rin ng pansin at pinagsikapang gumawa ng mga hakbang upang mapababa ang taripa ng kuryente ngayong buwan ng Hulyo.\nSa kabila nito, patuloy pa rin ang aming paalala na mahalagang maging masinop at matalino sa paggamit ng kuryente.\n#JulyPowerRate\n#ISELCO2"

b"POWER RATE UPDATE\n\nMagandang balita!\n\nIpatutupad ngayong buwan ng Hunyo 2023 ang pagbaba ng power rate mula sa Php 15.6878/kWh noong nakaraang buwan ay bumaba sa Php 15.3366/kwh para sa residential consumers. Mula naman sa Php 14.4975/kWh ay bumaba ito ngayong buwan sa Php 14.1463/kwh para sa low voltage consumers. Habang ang singil sa high voltage consumers ay bumaba ngayong buwan mula Php 13.0738/kWh sa Php12.7432/kwh.\n\nSa kabila ng abalang iskedyul ng pamunuan ng ISELCO II dahil sa iba't ibang nakahanay na aktibidad ng Kooperatiba, sa pamumuno ni Acting General Manager, Engr. Erni G. Baggao, ay pinagtuunan pa rin ng pansin at pinagsikapang gumawa ng mga hakbang upang mapababa ang taripa ng kuryente ngayong buwan ng Hunyo.\n\nSa kabila nito, patuloy pa rin ang aming paalala na mahalagang maging masinop at matalino sa paggamit ng kuryente.\n#JunePowerRate\n#ISELCO2"

b'A joint inspection of all substations in the service area of ISELCO II was conducted on May 24, 2023 by representatives from the Energy Regulatory Commission (ERC) and ISELCO II area Engineers.\n\nThe substation inspection was carried out to review and assess the actual demands of the Cooperative as a mandatory measure in relation to its CAPEX projects filed before the Energy Regulatory Commission.\n\nSubstations are crucial components of the distribution system that serve several important functions. Substations need to be maintained properly by Distribution Utilities to ensure that they are safe and operationally efficient in delivering power flow to commercial, residential, and industrial consumers.\n\nFollowing the completion of the inspection, the inspectors held an exit conference to discuss the findings, observations and overall conclusions from the work as well as any relevant recommendations from the Commission.\n#ERC\n#ISELCO2'

b"POWER RATE UPDATE\n\nMagandang balita!\n\nIpatutupad ngayong buwan ng Mayo 2023 ang pagbaba ng power rate mula sa Php 17.1080/kWh noong nakaraang buwan ay bumaba sa Php 15.6878/kwh para sa residential consumers. Mula naman sa Php 15.9177/kWh ay bumaba ito ngayong buwan sa Php 14.4975/kwh para sa low voltage consumers. Habang ang singil sa high voltage consumers ay bumaba ngayong buwan mula Php 14.008/kWh sa Php13.0738/kwh.\n\nSa kabila ng abalang iskedyul ng pamunuan ng ISELCO II dahil sa iba't ibang nakahanay na aktibidad ng Kooperatiba, sa pamumuno ni Acting General Manager, Engr. Erni G. Baggao, ay pinagtuunan pa rin ng pansin at pinagsikapang gumawa ng mga hakbang upang mapababa ang taripa ng kuryente ngayong buwan ng Mayo.\n\nSa kabila nito, patuloy pa rin ang aming paalala na mahalagang maging masinop at matalino sa paggamit ng kuryente.\n#MayPowerRate\n#ISELCO2"

b'ATING ALAMIN\n"Lifeline Rate Discount"\n\nAlinsunod sa Seksyon 3 ng Republic Act No. 11552, na pinamagatang \xe2\x80\x9cAn Act Extending and Enhancing the Implementation of the Lifeline Rate, amending for the Purpose, Section 73 of Republic Act No. 9136, otherwise known as the \xe2\x80\x9cElectric Power Industry Reform Act of 2001,\xe2\x80\x9d as amended by Republic Act No. 10150,\xe2\x80\x9d magbibigay ang gobyerno ng karagdagang subsidy para sa mga kwalipikadong low-income consumers.\n\nAng Lifeline Rate ay tumutukoy sa subsidized na rate na ibinibigay sa mga kwalipikadong marginalized end-users. Ang lifeline discount ay isang non-cash monetary discount na ilalapat ng distribution utility sa buwanang singil sa kuryente ng mga kwalipikadong residential consumers.\n#ISELCO2'

b"Today, March 24, 2023, the Isabela II Electric Cooperative (ISELCO II) joins the opening activity and virtual get-together of all women leaders and employees of Electric Cooperatives nationwide for a simultaneous celebration of National Womens Month, initiated by the Philippine Rural Electric Cooperatives Association (PHILRECA) via Zoom Meeting.\n\nIn line with the occasion, ISELCO II hosted a seminar for the female employees. There were three themes covered in the discussion. The discussion on Women's Reproductive Health was facilitated by Dr. Nancy Margarrette Roxas, Dr. Jhoanne Eizle Peralta-Ibanez, and Dr. Christina Calagui-Damaso from the Cagayan Valley Medical Center. Additionally, PMAJ. Ammy Dela Cruz Mawirat discussed relevant topics on Women's Rights. The seminar concluded with a discussion on Gender Sensitivity, which was led by Ms. Charmiya Rosalina Cruz.\n\nThe main objective of the seminar is to prepare women with adequate knowledge about Health, Dignity, and Role of a women in the present.\n\nEngr. Erni G. Baggao, Acting General Manager provided his entire support, which enabled the activity to take place.\n#NationalWomensMonth2023\n#ISELCO2"

b'Alinsunod sa Resolution No. 003 series of 2023 na aprubado noong 39th AGMA na ginanap nitong nakaraang Enero 29, 2023, ipinababatid ng pamunuan ng ISELCO II na simula buwan ng Marso billing 2023:\n\n     \xe2\x80\xa2 Mabibigyan ng 1% na diskwento ang mga Member-\n       Consumer-Owners (MCOs) na kumukonsumo ng 101 KWH\n       pataas at ang mga makakapagbabayad ng kanilang power bill\n       limang (5) araw pagkatapos ng reading at billing.\n\n    \xe2\x80\xa2 Mapapatawan ng 3% penalty ang mga MCOs na hindi\n      nakapagbayad sa due date.\n\n    \xe2\x80\xa2 Ang mga MCOs na kumokonsumo ng 100 KWH pababa ay\n      walang matatanggap na diskwento at hindi rin mapapatawan\n      ng penalty.\n\nTANDAAN: Lahat ng mga MCOs na hindi makapagbayad ng kanilang buwanang konsumo ay puputulan ng serbisyo sa kuryente alinsunod sa Policy on Disconnection.\n\nMaraming salamat po.'
b'POWER RATE UPDATE\n\nMagandang balita!\n\nMuling bumaba ang power rate na ipatutupad ngayong buwan ng Pebrero 2023. Mula sa Php 16.7099/kWh noong Enero ay bumaba sa Php16.3005/kwh para sa residential consumers. Mula naman sa Php15.5196/kWh ay bumaba ito ngayong buwan sa Php15.1102/kwh para sa low voltage consumers. Habang ang singil sa high voltage consumers ay bumaba ngayong buwan mula Php13.5558/kWh sa Php13.1132/kwh.\n\nPaalala na mahalagang maging masinop at matalino sa mga bagay na ating ginagamit lalo na sa kuryente.\n\n#PowerRateUpdate\n#ISELCO2\n#February2023'

b"The 39th ISELCO II Annual General Membership Assembly (AGMA) was successfully held last January 29, 2023 at the Ilagan Community Center, City of Ilagan, Isabela.\n\nA total of 8,688 MCOs from various municipalities under the purview of the Cooperative attended and participated in the official agenda. \n\nCity of Ilagan Mayor Josemarie L. Diaz and members of the Sangguniang Panlungsod were in attendance and supported the occasion.\n\nThe main objective of the event was to provide updates on its Financial, Institutional, and Technical operations for the Calendar Year 2022. \n\nMCOs were given the opportunity to express their concerns in an open forum following the presentation.\n\nChairman of the Board of Directors Hardy V. Urma, and Acting General Manager Erni G. Baggao took the lead in resolving matters raised and answering inquiries.\n\nAlongside with the reports, Election Committee and Audit Committee directors were also chosen. Member-Consumer Owners were given the opportunity to exercise their right to elect and select the people they wanted to post in the said committees.\n\nPrior to the program's conclusion, two tricycle units were raffled off as grand prize in an electronic raffle as appreciation to the MCOs who made an effort to take part in the assembly.\n\nThe ISELCO II Management and Board of Directors would like to express its sincerest gratitude to all those who supported and attended this annual event.\n#ISELCO2\n#39thAnnualGeneralMembershipAssembly"

b'POWER RATE UPDATE\n\nMagandang balita!\n\nMuling bumaba ang power rate na ipatutupad ngayong buwan ng Enero 2023. Mula sa Php 17.3606/ kWh noong Disyembre ay bumaba sa Php16.7099/kwh para sa residential consumers. Mula naman sa Php 16.1703/ kWh ay bumaba ito ngayong buwan sa Php15.5196/kwh para sa low voltage consumers. Habang ang singil sa high voltage consumers ay bumaba ngayong buwan mula Php 14.2908/ kWh sa Php13.5558/kwh.\n\nPaalala na mahalagang maging masinop at matalino sa mga bagay na ating ginagamit lalo na sa kuryente.'

b'On October 23\xe2\x80\x9326, 2022, the Philippine Federation of Electric Cooperatives (PHILFECO) hosted a seminar on "EC Organizational Restructuring and Realignment in conformity with EPIRA Demands and ERC Guidelines    and Requirements." The seminar was attended by representatives from ISELCO II including Mr. Benaldbert Bautista, Branch Manager, Ms. Apryl Cubangbang, MSD Chief, Engineer Harold David, LCOMD Chief, and Ms. Mary Claire Valencia, Information Officer.\n\nThe seminar\'s main objective was to prepare Electric Cooperatives (ECs) with  adequate knowledge about the fundamentals of organizational restructuring and functional realignment that will help ECs adapt to the service demands and impending changes brought on by the open access and retail competition environment envisioned by EPIRA, as well as the implementation of the ERC-mandated separation and unbundling plan for all parties in the electric power industry.\n\nR.A. 9136, otherwise known as the Electric Power Industry Reform Act (EPIRA) of 2001 provides a framework for the restructuring of the electric power industry.\n\nThe seminar encouraged its member ECs to review and reassess their vision, mission, and goals to make sure they remain consistent with the demands of EPIRA. Additionally, the seminar emphasized the importance of restructuring and reorganization to ensure that the ECs\' current organizational structures remain applicable to their present operations.\n#ISELCO2'

b'POWER RATES UPDATE \n\nIpinapabatid sa mga Member-Consumer-Owners (MCOs) ang pagtaas sa power rate ngayong buwan ng Nobyembre 2022. Ito ay epekto ng mataas na generation charge mula sa mga plantang pinagkukuhanan ng supply ng kuryente ng ating Kooperatiba.\n\nBinibigyang-diin na ang generation charge ay isang pass-through charge na hindi napupunta sa Kooperatiba kundi sa mga power suppliers. Tinitiyak ng Kooperatiba na ang ating power rate ay alinsunod sa mga regulasyon ng Energy Regulatory Commission (ERC).\n\nBatid ng Kooperatiba ang inyong malawak na pang-unawa.\n\nMaraming Salamat po.\n\n#ISELCO2\n#ISELCO2PowerRate\n#PowerRateNovember2022'

b'POWER RATES UPDATE \n\nIpinapabatid sa mga member-consumer-owners na ang pagtaas sa power rate ngayong buwan ng Oktubre 2022 ay epekto ng mataas na generation charges mula sa mga plantang pinagkukuhanan ng supply ng kuryente ng ating Kooperatiba.\n\nBinibigyang-diin na ang generation charge ay isang pass-through charge na hindi napupunta sa Kooperatiba kundi sa mga power providers. Tinitiyak ng Kooperatiba na ang ating power rate ay alinsunod sa mga regulasyon ng Energy Regulatory Commission (ERC).\n\nBatid ng Kooperatiba ang inyong malawak na pang-unawa. Maraming Salamat po.\n#PowerRateUpdate\n#ISELCO2'

b"The Philippine Rural Electric Cooperatives Association recently held the 2022 PHILRECA Convention and 43rd Annual General Membership Meeting (AGMM) on August 10-12, 2022 with the theme: \xe2\x80\x9cLEAVING NO ONE BEHIND: Achieving Social Equitability through Rural Electrification and Empowerment of Filipino Communities.\xe2\x80\x9d\n\nThe association presented the 2022 PHILRECA Awards from the Wires to the Electric Cooperatives (ECs), officers, employees, and honored guests during the three-day convention in recognition of their outstanding work toward total rural electrification and sustainable rural development. The awards were based on validated data gathered from the Electric Cooperatives as well as from the Energy Regulatory Commission (ERC).\n\nISELCO II received the following Plaques and Certificates of Recognition:\n\nBright Beginning Award for an exemplary performance in the pursuit of total electrification and sustainable rural development during extraordinary times notwithstanding all difficulties confronting the rural electrification movement.\n\nPrompt Payor Award for committing itself to timely and efficient settlement of its annual dues as a member of PHILRECA.\n\nStrong Commitment to Brotherhood Award for its unwavering support and upholding the true spirit of bayanihan in helping ECs and member-consumer-owners during typhoon Odette through the PHILRECA Task Force Kapatid.\n\nLimelight Award for being the front runner in the pursuit total electrification and sustainable rural development notwithstanding all challenges confronting the rural electrification movement.\n\nExtra Mile Award for implementing the Pantawid Liwanag Program 4, an initiative in partnership with government frontline agencies aimed to uplift the lives of the MCOs and mitigate the impact these challenging times. \n\nMCO Champ Award for having organized its member-consumer-owners in the barangay level, and for empowering the MCOs of ISELCO II to become advocates of the rural electrification movement.\n\nOutstanding Radio Program Excellence Award in recognition of the efforts to establish a radio program that exemplify commitment to community service, genuine and accurate news and information.\n\nUnparalleled Service Award for ensuring that EC employees are responsive and efficient in handling EC-related concerns through the operationalization of the 24/7 customer service to member-consumer-owners.\n\nISELCO II dedicates these awards to all of its member-consumer-owners who serve as the Coop's foundation as it strives to achieve further milestones in the years to come.\n\nOn the other hand, the National Electrification Administration (NEA) released Memorandum 2022-33 on July 13, 2022, stating the EC Overall Performance Assessment and Size Classification for the year 2021, in which ISELCO II, a Mega Large EC, remained Category A. ISELCO II has been an A Category EC since the year 2018.\n\nECs are evaluated yearly to ensure they are fully compliant with the Key Performance Standards (KPS) of NEA based on four parameters: Financial, Institutional, Technical, and Reportorial Requirements.\n#TheWires\n#PHILRECA\n#ISELCO2"

b'Ipinapabatid sa mga member-consumer-owners ang pagtaas ng singilin sa kuryente na ipatutupad ngayong buwan ng Agosto 2022. Php16.7771/kwh para sa mga residential consumers, Php15.5868/kwh sa Low voltage, Php9.1283/kwh sa SPUG-Palanan at Php13.7884/kwh sa High voltage.\nMalaking epekto ang pagtaas ng generation rate mula sa mga plantang pinagkukuhanan ng supply ng kuryente ng ISELCO II. Ito ay bunsod pa rin ng pagtaas ng presyo ng coal sa world market. Ang coal ay ginagamit ng mga power plants sa pag-generate ng kuryente.\nBatid ng Kooperatiba ang inyong malawak na pang-unawa. Maraming Salamat po.\n#Iselco2\n#AugustPowerRate'

b'Tunghayan po natin ngayong araw August 10, 2022 sa ganap na 1:00 pm ang Facebook Live ng ating Kooperatiba upang bigyang-kasagutan ang mga madalas na katanungan ng Member-Consumers.\nAng mga live viewers ay maaaring makilahok sa Trivia Questions na gaganapin sa FB Live upang manalo ng mga pa-premyo. \nKindly like and share.\n#Iselco2\n#Iselco2Hour'
b"On July 31, 2022, ISELCO II hosted its Synchronized 38th Annual General Membership Assembly (AGMA) at Ragan Sur Community Center in Delfin Albano, Isabela, and the Quezon Coliseum in Samonte Quezon, Isabela. ISELCO II conducted its annual affair in two venues simultaneously by means of teleconferencing aiming to accommodate a broader number of MCOs both from the Southern and Northern part of its coverage area.  The election of the Audit Committee and Election Committee members also took place concurrently with AGMA. To accommodate member-consumers, computerized registration was used to validate and register participants as early as 8:00 in the morning.\n\nThe annual event is organized each year for the member-consumer-owners with the aim of reporting the Cooperative's Financial, Institutional, and Technical operations in the previous year. A month before the event, ISELCO II intensified its information campaign to alert member-consumers. This included using tarpaulins posted in public spaces, public address, radio commercials, bill inserts, Facebook postings, and Facebook Live, text blasts, letters to LNB presidents, SP members, to mention a few.\n\nISELCO II recognizes PNP Delfin Albano and PNP Quezon for helping to keep the event in good order and tranquility. First-aid stations were set up by rescue teams from Delfin Albano and Quezon to handle appropriate medical emergencies on site. Both Ragan Sur National High School and Delfin Albano High School students entertained the audience with performances of their talents.\n\nThe outstanding Barangay Power Association (BAPA) that maintained the sustainability of the association in their area was once again recognized at this year's assembly.  The AGMA is expected to be a great public platform for discussion and clarification of issues relating to ISELCO II operations. However, the number of attendees present at the event fell short of the necessary quorum to proceed with the business proper. Nonetheless, the Cooperative expresses gratitude to the member-consumers who attended the said event."

The said awards were received by Board Chairman, Director Walfrido G. Binag and OIC General Manager, Mr.Charles Roy B. b'\xe2\x80\xbc\xef\xb8\x8f POWER RATES UPDATE \xe2\x80\xbc\xef\xb8\x8f\n\nIpinapabatid sa mga member-consumer-owners ang pagtaas ng singilin sa kuryente na ipatutupad ngayong buwan ng Hulyo 2022. Php15.9390/kwh para sa mga residential consumers, Php14.7487/kwh sa Low voltage, at Php13.0402/kwh sa High voltage.\n\nMalaking epekto ang pagtaas ng generation rate mula sa mga plantang pinagkukuhanan ng supply ng kuryente ng ISELCO II. Ito ay bunsod pa rin ng pagtaas ng presyo ng coal sa world market. Ang coal ay ginagamit ng mga power plants sa pag-generate ng kuryente.\n\nBatid ng Kooperatiba ang inyong malawak na pang-unawa. Maraming Salamat po.\n#Iselco2'

b'Ang ISELCO II ay opisyal na rehistrado sa Cooperative Development Authority (CDA) noong June 22, 2007. Alinsunod sa Rule 10, Section 3 ng RA 9520; Article VII, Section 6 ng Cooperative By-Laws at Articles of Cooperation - Article 10, ang paglalagak ng share capital ng bawat MCO ay naipatupad upang maging regular na miyembro at ganap na kamay \xe2\x80\x93 ari ng kooperatiba.\n\n Ang regular na Member-Consumer-Owners o MCOs ay kailangang maglagak ng labing dalawang (12) share capital na nagkakahalaga ng P100 bawat share. Sa kabuuan, ito ay nagkakahalaga ng \xe2\x82\xb11,200.00 para sa 12 shares. \n Ang capital share na \xe2\x82\xb11,200 ay naibabawas ayon sa sumusunod na nakunsumo sa bawat buwan hanggang sa ito ay makumpleto:\n 1-20KWH          \xe2\x82\xb120.00\n 21-50KWH         \xe2\x82\xb150.00\n 51KWH pataas \xe2\x82\xb1100.00 \n\n Sa mga MCOs na ganap nang nagbayad ng kanilang CAPITAL SHARES noong December 2018, ang DIVIDEND ay na-credit sa iyong account at itinuring bilang bayad o paunang bayad sa mga singil sa kuryente ng mga consumers na WALANG ARREARS. \n\n I-click ang link na ito https://www.facebook.com/ISELCOII/photos/a.368453126506226/5564359653582188/ upang makita ang schedule ng mga DIVIDENDS na naibigay at naibawas sa power bill ng mga MCO simula January 2022.\n\n Para sa iba pang katanungan hinggil dito, tumawag sa ISELCO II hotline: Globe 0956 994 6944  /  Smart 0929 663 4511.'

Urma ang iba pang empleyado ng ISELCO II katulad ni Mr. Benaldbert Bautista, Aurora Branch Office Manager; Ms. Apryl Cubangbang, MSD Chief; Ms. Genevieve Uy, MSDMR Section Head; at Ms. Mary Claire Valencia, Information Officer. \n\nUmaasa naman ang kooperatiba na maging bahagi pa rin ito ng iba pang klaseng pagpupulong kaharap ang mismong mga member-consumer-owners upang mas lalo pa nilang maunawaan ang mga bagay patungkol sa kooperatiba.'
b'Sa paglalayong makapagbigay ng wastong impormasyon patungkol sa operasyon ng ISELCO II ay dinaluhan ng mga kawani nito ang pagpupulong ng mga Sangguniang Bayan members sa Aurora, Isabela noong ika-15 ng Nobyembre, 2021.\n\nSa naturang pagpupulong, naibahagi sa mga municipal councilors ang mga programa at aktibidades ng ISELCO II sa kasalukuyan. Dagdag pa rito, natalakay din ang batas na RA 11361 o Anti-Obstruction of Power Lines Act, mga sanhi ng power outages, at iba pa. Mahalagang maipaalam sa kanila ang mga bagay patungkol dito dahil bilang mga lingkod-bayan, kabilang sila sa mga nakatatanggap ng isyu at alalahanin ng mga member-consumer- owners pagdating sa usaping pangkuryente.\n\nKabilang sa mga dumalo sina  Director Hardy V. Urma ng District III, Ms. Pinky Ann C. Lucas, Institutional Services Department Manager at iba pang kawani ng ISELCO II.'
b'Sa pamamagitan ng Pantawid Liwanag Program 4 o PLP4 ay muling nakapagbahagi ng cash assistance para sa mga member-consumer-owners (MCOs) sa iba\xe2\x80\x99t ibang bahagi sa nasasakupan ng ISELCO II. Ginanap ang pamamahagi ng tulong pinansyal ng tatlong magkakasunod na araw mula Nobyembre 11-13, 2021. \n\nAng programang ito ay pinangunahan ng PHILRECA, sa tulong ng DSWD at ISELCO II. Sa kabuuan, 324 na MCOs ang nakatanggap ng tulong mula sa PLP4. Matatandaan na nagsimula ang programa noong nakaraang taon upang makatulong sa mga MCOs sa panahon ng pandemya.\n\nSanib pwersa ang mga opisyal ng ISELCO I, ISELCO II at PHILRECA sa pamamahagi ng tulong na nagpakita ng pagkakaisa ng mga kooperatiba sa bansa.'
